<t>CREATE TABLE compliance_regulations (
  regulation_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  regulation_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL
);


CREATE TABLE compliance_documents (
  document_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  document_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  regulation_id INT,
  FOREIGN KEY (regulation_id) REFERENCES compliance_regulations(regulation_id)
);


CREATE TABLE compliance_issues (
  issue_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
  issue_description TEXT NOT NULL,
  document_id INT,
  FOREIGN KEY (document_id) REFERENCES compliance_documents(document_id)
);

CREATE TABLE compliance_policies (policy_id INT PRIMARY KEY, policy_name TEXT, description TEXT);

CREATE TABLE user_profiles (user_id INT PRIMARY KEY, full_name TEXT, email TEXT, phone_number TEXT);

CREATE TABLE compliance_reports (report_id INT PRIMARY KEY, report_date DATE, policy_id INT, user_id INT);</t><s>insert into user_profiles (user_id, full_name, email, phone_number) values (1, 'john doe', 'john.doe@example.com', '123-456-7890') on conflict (user_id) do update set full_name = excluded.full_name, email = excluded.email, phone_number = excluded.phone_number;</s>
